</TABLE>
<P class="p729 ft12">DIRECTIVE 2007/47/EC OF THE EUROPEAN PARLIAMENT AND OF THE COUNCIL</P>
<P class="p730 ft12">of 5 September 2007</P>
<P class="p248 ft12">amending Council Directive 90/385/EEC on the approximation of the laws of the Member States relating to active implantable medical devices, Council Directive 93/42/EEC concerning medical devices and Directive 98/8/EC concerning the placing of biocidal products on the market</P>
<P class="p731 ft53">(Text with EEA relevance)</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<DIV id="id_2_1">
<P class="p250 ft23">THE EUROPEAN PARLIAMENT AND THE COUNCIL OF THE EUROPEAN UNION,</P>
<P class="p732 ft2">Having regard to the Treaty establishing the European Commu­ nity, and in particular Article 95 thereof,</P>
<P class="p86 ft2">Having regard to the proposal from the Commission,</P>
<P class="p733 ft2">Having regard to the opinion of the European Economic and Social Committee (<SPAN class="ft54">1</SPAN>),</P>
<P class="p734 ft2">Acting in accordance with the procedure laid down in Article 251 of the Treaty (<SPAN class="ft54">2</SPAN>),</P>
<P class="p86 ft2">Whereas:</P>
<P class="p735 ft27"><SPAN class="ft16">(1)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft55">Council Directive 93/42/EEC (</SPAN><SPAN class="ft56">3</SPAN>) requires the Commission to submit a report to the Council, no later than five years from the date of implementation of that Directive, concerning: (i) information on incidents occurring follow­ ing the placing of devices on the market, (ii) clinical investigation carried out in accordance with the procedure set out in Annex VIII to Directive 93/42/EEC, and (iii) design examination and EC type examination of medical devices that incorporate, as an integral part, a substance which, if used separately, may be considered to be a medicinal product as defined in Directive 2001/83/EC of the European Parliament and of the Council of 6 November 2001 on the Community code relating to medicinal products for human use (<SPAN class="ft56">4</SPAN>) and which is liable to act upon the body with action ancillary to that of the device.</P>
<P class="p736 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(2)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft49">The Commission brought forward the conclusions of that report in its Communication to the Council and the European Parliament on medical devices which, at the request of the Member States, was expanded to cover all aspects of the Community regulatory framework for medical devices.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p737 ft27"><SPAN class="ft16">(3)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft55">This Communication was welcomed by the Council in its Conclusions on medical devices of 2 December 2003 (</SPAN><SPAN class="ft56">5</SPAN>). It</P>
<P class="p521 ft23">(<SPAN class="ft54">1</SPAN>) OJ C 195, 18.8.2006, p. 14.</P>
<P class="p257 ft57">(<SPAN class="ft54">2</SPAN>) Opinion of the European Parliament of 29 March 2007 (not yet published in the Official Journal) and Council Decision of 23 July 2007.</P>
<P class="p257 ft57">(<SPAN class="ft54">3</SPAN>) OJ L 169, 12.7.1993, p. 1. Directive as last amended by Regulation (EC) No 1882/2003 of the European Parliament and of the Council (OJ L 284, 31.10.2003, p. 1).</P>
<P class="p257 ft57">(<SPAN class="ft54">4</SPAN>) OJ L 311, 28.11.2001, p. 67. Directive as last amended by Regulation (EC) No 1901/2006 of the European Parliament and of the Council (OJ L 378, 27.12.2006, p. 1).</P>
<P class="p738 ft23">(<SPAN class="ft54">5</SPAN>) OJ C 20, 24.1.2004, p. 1.</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p739 ft2">was also discussed by the European Parliament which on 3 June 2003 adopted a resolution on the health implications of Directive 93/42/EEC (<SPAN class="ft54">6</SPAN>).</P>
<P class="p740 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(4)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft49">Following from the conclusions drawn in that Commu­ nication it is necessary and appropriate to amend Council Directive 90/385/EEC (</SPAN><SPAN class="ft54">7</SPAN>), Directive 93/42/EEC and Direc­ tive 98/8/EC of the European Parliament and of the Council (<SPAN class="ft54">8</SPAN>).</P>
<P class="p741 ft27"><SPAN class="ft16">(5)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft55">To ensure consistency of interpretation and implementation between Directives 93/42/EEC and 90/385/EEC the legal framework related to issues such as authorised representa­ tive, the European databank, health protection measures, and the application of Directive 93/42/EEC as regards medical devices incorporating stable derivates of human blood or human plasma, as introduced by Directive 2000/ 70/EC (</SPAN><SPAN class="ft56">9</SPAN>), should be extended to Directive 90/385/EEC. The application of the provisions on medical devices incorpor­ ating stable derivates of human blood or human plasma includes application of Directive 2002/98/EC of the European Parliament and of the Council of 27 January 2003 setting standards of quality and safety for the collection, testing, processing, storage and distribution of human blood and blood components and amending Directive 2001/83/EC (<SPAN class="ft56">10</SPAN>).</P>
<P class="p742 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(6)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft49">It is necessary to clarify that software in its own right, when specifically intended by the manufacturer to be used for one or more of the medical purposes set out in the definition of a medical device, is a medical device. Software for general purposes when used in a healthcare setting is not a medical device.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p743 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(7)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft49">Particular care should be taken to ensure that the</SPAN></P>
<P class="p407 ft27">reprocessing of medical devices does not endanger patients’ safety or health. It is therefore necessary to provide clarification on the definition of the term ‘single use’, as well as to make provision for uniform labelling and</P>
<P class="p238 ft23">(<SPAN class="ft54">6</SPAN>) OJ C 68 E, 18.3.2004, p. 85.</P>
<P class="p744 ft23">(<SPAN class="ft54">7</SPAN>) OJ L 189, 20.7.1990, p. 17. Directive as last amended by Regulation (EC) No 1882/2003.</P>
<P class="p744 ft57">(<SPAN class="ft54">8</SPAN>) OJ L 123, 24.4.1998, p. 1. Directive as last amended by Commission Directive 2007/20/EC (OJ L 94, 4.4.2007, p. 23).</P>
<P class="p263 ft57">(<SPAN class="ft54">9</SPAN>) Directive 2000/70/EC of the European Parliament and of the Council of 16 November 2000 amending Council Directive 93/42/ EEC as regards medical devices incorporating stable derivates of human blood or human plasma (OJ L 313, 13.12.2000, p. 22).</P>
<P class="p16 ft23">(<SPAN class="ft54">10</SPAN>) OJ L 33, 8.2.2003, p. 30.</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_85">


<DIV id="id_1">
<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t22">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr2 td92"><SPAN class="p8 ft2">L 247/22</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr5 td93"><SPAN class="p76 ft2">EN</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr2 td108"><SPAN class="p728 ft2">Official Journal of the European Union</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr2 td109"><SPAN class="p10 ft2">21.9.2007</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr21 td96"><SPAN class="p8 ft34">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr21 td97"><SPAN class="p8 ft34">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr21 td110"><SPAN class="p8 ft34">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr21 td111"><SPAN class="p8 ft34">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<DIV id="id_2_1">
<P class="p745 ft2">instructions for use. Moreover, the Commission should engage in further analysis in order to see if additional measures are appropriate to ensure a high level of protection for patients.</P>
<P class="p269 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(8)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft49">In the light of technical innovation and the development of initiatives at the international level it is necessary to enhance the provisions on clinical evaluation, including clarification that clinical data is generally required for all devices regardless of classification and the possibility to centralise data on clinical investigations in the European databank.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p266 ft52"><SPAN class="ft16">(9)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft118">In order to provide clearer evidence of the compliance of </SPAN><NOBR>custom-made</NOBR> device manufacturers, an explicit requirement for a post market production review system involving incident reporting to authorities should be introduced, as is already in place for other devices, and to enhance patient information, a requirement should be introduced that the ‘Statement’ under Annex VIII to Directive 93/42/EEC should be available to the patient and that it should contain the name of the manufacturer.</P>
<P class="p267 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(10)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft62">In the light of technical progress in information technology and medical devices, a process should be provided to allow information supplied by the manufacturer to be available by other means.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p746 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(11)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft62">Manufacturers of Class I sterile and/or measuring medical devices should be given the option of using the full quality assurance conformity assessment module in order to provide them with more flexibility in the choice of compliance modules.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p269 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(12)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft62">In order to support market surveillance activities by Member States it is necessary and appropriate, in the case of implantable devices, to increase the time period for the retention of documents for administrative purposes to at least 15 years.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p747 ft27"><SPAN class="ft16">(13)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft64">For the appropriate and efficient functioning of Directive 93/42/EEC as regards regulatory advice on classification issues arising at national level, in particular on whether or not a product falls under the definition of a medical device, it is in the interest of national market surveillance and the health and safety of humans to establish a procedure for decisions on whether or not a product falls under the medical device definition.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p748 ft52"><SPAN class="ft16">(14)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft65">To ensure that, where a manufacturer does not have a registered place of business in the Community, authorities have a single individual person authorised by the manufacturer whom they can address in matters relating to the compliance of the devices with the Directives it is necessary to introduce an obligation for such manufacturers to designate an authorised representative for a device. This designation should be effective at least for all devices of the same model.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p749 ft27"><SPAN class="ft16">(15)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft64">To further ensure public health and safety it is necessary to provide for a more consistent application of the provisions on health protection measures. Particular care should be taken to ensure that, when in use, the products do not endanger patients’ health or safety.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p268 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(16)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft62">In support of transparency in Community legislation, certain information related to medical devices and their conformity with Directive 93/42/EEC, in particular infor­ mation on registration, on vigilance reports and on certificates, should be available to any interested party and the general public.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p750 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(17)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft62">To better coordinate the application and efficiency of national resources when applied to issues related to Directive 93/42/EEC, the Member States should cooperate with each other and at international level.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p751 ft52"><SPAN class="ft16">(18)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft65">As design for patient safety initiatives play an increasing role in public health policy, it is necessary to expressly set out the need to consider ergonomic design in the essential requirements. In addition the level of training and knowl­ edge of the user, such as in the case of a lay user, should be further emphasised within the essential requirements. The manufacturer should place particular emphasis on the consequences of misuse of the product and its adverse effects on the human body.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p752 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(19)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft62">In the light of experience gained regarding activities of both the notified bodies and the authorities in the assessment of devices which require intervention of the appropriate authorities for medicines and human blood derivatives their duties and tasks should be clarified.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p753 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(20)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft62">Taking account of the growing importance of software in the field of medical devices, be it as stand alone or as software incorporated in a device, validation of software in accordance with the state of the art should be an essential requirement.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p753 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(21)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft62">In the light of the increased use of third Parties to carry out the design and manufacture of devices on behalf of the manufacturer, it is important that the manufacturer demonstrates that he applies adequate controls to the third party to continue to ensure the efficient operating of the quality system.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p754 ft61"><SPAN class="ft16">(22)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft63">The classification rules are based on the vulnerability of the human body taking account of the potential risks associated with the technical design and manufacture of the devices. Explicit prior authorisation with regard to conformity, including an assessment of the design documentation, is required for Class III devices to be placed on the market. In performing its duties under the quality assurance and verification conformity assessment modules for all other classes of devices, it is essential and necessary for a notified body, in order to be assured of the</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_86">
<DIV id="p86dimg1">
<INGENBILD zsrc="GW0310586x1.jpg/" id="p86img1">
</DIV>


<DIV id="id_1">
<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t22">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr2 td92"><SPAN class="p244 ft2">21.9.2007</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr5 td93"><SPAN class="p76 ft2">EN</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr2 td94"><SPAN class="p728 ft2">Official Journal of the European Union</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr2 td95"><SPAN class="p8 ft2">L 247/23</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr21 td96"><SPAN class="p8 ft34">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr21 td97"><SPAN class="p8 ft34">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr21 td98"><SPAN class="p8 ft34">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr21 td99"><SPAN class="p8 ft34">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<DIV id="id_2_1">
<P class="p279 ft27">compliance of the manufacturer with Directive 93/42/EEC, to review the design documentation for the medical device. The depth and extent of this review should be commensu­ rate with the classification of the device, the novelty of the intended treatment, the degree of intervention, the novelty of the technology or construction materials, and the complexity of the design and/or technology. This review can be achieved by taking a representative example of design documentation of one or more type(s) of devices from those being manufactured. Further review(s), and in particular the assessment of changes to the design that could affect conformity with the essential requirements, should be part of the surveillance activities of the notified body.</P>
<P class="p755 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(23)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft62">It is necessary to remove the incoherence in the classification rules as a result of which invasive devices with respect to body orifices intended for connection to an active Class I medical device were not classified.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p756 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(24)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft62">The measures necessary for the implementation of Directive 90/385/EEC and Directive 93/42/EEC should be adopted in accordance with Council Decision 1999/468/EC of 28 June 1999 laying down the procedures for the exercise of implementing powers conferred on the Commission (</SPAN><SPAN class="ft54">1</SPAN>).</P>
<P class="p757 ft52"><SPAN class="ft16">(25)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft65">In particular, power should be conferred on the Commis­ sion to adapt classification rules for medical devices, to adapt the means by which the information needed to use medical devices safely and properly may be set out, to determine conditions for making certain information publicly available, to adapt the provisions on clinical investigations set out in certain Annexes, to adopt particular requirements for placing certain medical devices on the market or putting them into service, and to take decisions to withdraw such devices from the market for reasons of protection of health or safety. Since those measures are of general scope and are designed to amend or supplement Directive 90/385/EEC and Directive 93/42/EEC by the modification or addition of </SPAN><NOBR>non-essential</NOBR> elements, they must be adopted in accordance with the regulatory procedure with scrutiny provided for in Article 5a of Decision 1999/468/EC.</P>
<P class="p758 ft61"><SPAN class="ft16">(26)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft63">When, on imperative grounds of urgency, the normal time limits for the regulatory procedure with scrutiny cannot be complied with, the Commission should be able to use the urgency procedure provided for in Article 5a(6) of Decision 1999/468/EC for taking decisions on withdrawal of certain medical devices from the market and for the adoption of particular requirements for placing such devices on the market or putting them into service for reasons of protection of health or safety.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p759 ft23">(<SPAN class="ft54">1</SPAN>) OJ L 184, 17.7.1999, p. 23. Decision as amended by Decision 2006/ 512/EC (OJ L 200, 22.7.2006, p. 11).</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p258 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(27)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft62">The Commission should give a mandate to CEN and/or Cenelec to specify technical requirements and a suitable specific label for </SPAN><NOBR>phthalate-containing</NOBR> devices within 12 months after entry into force of this Directive.</P>
<P class="p285 ft27"><SPAN class="ft16">(28)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft64">Many Member States have established recommendations with the aim of reducing or limiting the use of medical devices containing critical phthalates on children, pregnant and nursing women and other patients at risk. To enable medical professionals to avoid such risks, devices which possibly release phthalates to the body of the patient should be labelled accordingly.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p760 ft27"><SPAN class="ft16">(29)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft64">In accordance with the essential requirements on the design and manufacture of medical devices, manufacturers should avoid the use of substances that may possibly compromise the health of patients, in particular of substances which are carcinogenic, mutagenic or toxic to reproduction, and should, as appropriate, strive to develop alternative substances or products with a lower risk potential.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p761 ft27"><SPAN class="ft16">(30)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft64">It should be clarified that alongside Directives 90/385/EEC and 93/42/EEC, in vitro diagnostic medical devices, which are the subject of Directive 98/79/EC of the European Parliament and of the Council of 27 October 1998 on in vitro diagnostic medical devices (</SPAN><SPAN class="ft56">2</SPAN>), should also be excluded from the scope of Directive 98/8/EC.</P>
<P class="p762 ft27"><SPAN class="ft16">(31)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft64">In accordance with point 34 of the Interinstitutional agreement on better </SPAN><NOBR>law-making</NOBR> (<SPAN class="ft56">3</SPAN>), Member States are encouraged to draw up, for themselves and in the interests of the Community, their own tables illustrating, as far as possible, the correlation between this Directive and the transposition measures, and to make them public.</P>
<P class="p763 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(32)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft62">Directives 90/385/EEC, 93/42/EEC and 98/8/EC should therefore be amended accordingly,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p132 ft23">HAVE ADOPTED THIS DIRECTIVE:</P>
<P class="p764 ft3">Article 1</P>
<P class="p765 ft2">Directive 90/385/EEC is hereby amended as follows:</P>
<P class="p140 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft66">Article 1 shall be amended as follows:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p334 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft73">paragraph 2 shall be amended as follows:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p397 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(i)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft66">point (a) shall be replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p482 ft27">‘(a) “medical device” means any instrument, apparatus, appliance, software, material or other article, whether used alone or in combination, together with any accessories, including the software intended by its</P>
<P class="p766 ft23">(<SPAN class="ft54">2</SPAN>) OJ L 331, 7.12.1998, p. 1. Directive as last amended by Regulation (EC) No 1882/2003.</P>
<P class="p16 ft23">(<SPAN class="ft54">3</SPAN>) OJ C 321, 31.12.2003, p. 1.</P>

	<TD class="tr2 td108"><SPAN class="p728 ft2">Official Journal of the European Union</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr2 td109"><SPAN class="p10 ft2">21.9.2007</SPAN> </TD>

	<TD class="tr21 td96"><SPAN class="p8 ft34">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr21 td97"><SPAN class="p8 ft34">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr21 td110"><SPAN class="p8 ft34">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr21 td111"><SPAN class="p8 ft34">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>

</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<DIV id="id_2_1">
<P class="p767 ft2">manufacturer to be used specifically for diagnostic and/or therapeutic purposes and necessary for its proper application, intended by the manufacturer to be used for human beings for the purpose of:</P>
<P class="p768 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">—</SPAN><SPAN class="ft49">diagnosis, prevention, monitoring, treatment or alleviation of disease,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p769 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">—</SPAN><SPAN class="ft49">diagnosis, monitoring, treatment, alle­ viation of or compensation for an injury or handicap,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p769 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">—</SPAN><SPAN class="ft49">investigation, replacement or modifi­ cation of the anatomy or of a physiological process,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p298 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">—</SPAN><SPAN class="ft49">control of conception,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p770 ft2">and which does not achieve its principal intended action in or on the human body by pharmacological, immunological or metabolic means, but which may be assisted in its function by such means;’</P>
<P class="p771 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(ii)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft49">points (d), (e) and (f) shall be replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p352 ft2">the labelling, in the instructions and/or in promotional material;’</P>
<P class="p212 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(iii)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft85">the following points shall be added:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p772 ft52">‘(j) “authorised representative” means any nat­ ural or legal person established in the Community who, explicitly designated by the manufacturer, acts and may be addressed by authorities and bodies in the Community instead of the manufacturer with regard to the latter's obligations under this Directive;</P>
<P class="p773 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(k)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft49">“clinical data” means the safety and/or performance information that is generated from the use of a device. Clinical data are sourced from:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p774 ft2"><SPAN class="ft27">—</SPAN><SPAN class="ft49">clinical investigation(s) of the device concerned, or</SPAN></P>
<P class="p775 ft2"><SPAN class="ft27">—</SPAN><SPAN class="ft49">clinical investigation(s) or other stu­ dies reported in the scientific litera­ ture, of a similar device for which equivalence to the device in question can be demonstrated, or</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_3">
<DIV id="id_3_1">
<P class="p776 ft61">‘(d) <NOBR>“custom-made</NOBR> device” means any device specifically made in accordance with a duly qualified medical practitioner's written pre­ scription which gives, under his responsi­ bility, specific design characteristics and is intended for the sole use of a particular patient. <NOBR>Mass-produced</NOBR> devices which need to be adapted to meet the specific require­ ments of the medical practitioner or any other professional user shall not be con­ sidered to be <NOBR>custom-made</NOBR> devices;</P>
<P class="p281 ft27"><SPAN class="ft16">(e)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft55">“device intended for clinical investigation” means any device intended for use by a duly qualified medical practitioner when conducting clinical investigations as referred to in Section 2.1 of Annex 7 in an adequate human clinical environment.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p777 ft27">For the purpose of conducting clinical investigation, any other person who, by virtue of his professional qualifications, is authorised to carry out such investigation shall be accepted as equivalent to a duly qualified medical practitioner;</P>
<P class="p778 ft27"><SPAN class="ft16">(f)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft93">“intended purpose” means the use for which the device is intended according to the data supplied by the manufacturer on</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_3_2">
<P class="p779 ft2"><SPAN class="ft27">—</SPAN><SPAN class="ft49">published and/or unpublished reports on other clinical experience of either the device in question or a similar device for which equivalence to the device in question can be demon­ strated.’;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p402 ft2"><SPAN class="ft23">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft49">paragraph 3 shall be replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p780 ft52">‘3. Where an active implantable medical device is intended to administer a substance defined as a medicinal product within the meaning of Article 1 of Directive 2001/83/EC (*), that device shall be gov­ erned by this Directive, without prejudice to the provisions of Directive 2001/83/EC with regard to the medicinal product.</P>
<P class="p781 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(*)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft73">OJ L 311, 28.11.2001, p. 67. Directive as last amended by Regulation (EC) No 1901/2006 (OJ L 378, 27.12.2006, p. 1)’</SPAN></P>
<P class="p212 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft73">paragraph 4 shall be replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p782 ft27">‘4. Where an active implantable medical device incorporates, as an integral part, a substance which, if used separately, may be considered to be a medicinal product within the meaning of Article 1 of Directive 2001/83/EC and which is liable to act upon the</P>

<P class="p317 ft2">human body with action that is ancillary to that of the device, that device shall be evaluated and authorised in accordance with this Directive.’;</P>
<P class="p107 ft2"><SPAN class="ft23">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft86">the following paragraph shall be inserted:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p783 ft61">‘4a. <P class="p786 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(*)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft73">Directive 2004/108/EC of the European Parlia­ ment and of the Council of 15 December 2004 on the approximation of the laws of the Member States relating to electromagnetic compatibility (OJ L 390, 31.12.2004, p. 24).’;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p107 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(f)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft80">the following paragraph shall be added:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p787 ft2">‘6. This Directive shall not apply to:</P>
<P class="p788 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft73">medicinal products covered by Directive 2001/ 83/EC. In deciding whether a product falls under that Directive or this Directive, particular account shall be taken of the principal mode of action of the product;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p789 ft27"><SPAN class="ft23">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft78">human blood, blood products, plasma or blood cells of human origin or to devices which incorporate at the time of placing on the market such blood products, plasma or cells with the exception of devices referred to in paragraph 4a;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p789 ft27"><SPAN class="ft16">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft75">transplants or tissues or cells of human origin or to products incorporating or derived from tissues or cells of human origin, with the exception of devices referred to in paragraph 4a;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p790 ft27"><SPAN class="ft16">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft55">transplants or tissues or cells of animal origin, unless a device is manufactured utilising animal tissue which is rendered </SPAN><NOBR>non-viable</NOBR> or non­ viable products derived from animal tissue.’;</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p16 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft66">Article 2 shall be replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p791 ft3">‘Article 2</P>
<P class="p328 ft2">Member States shall take all necessary steps to ensure that the devices may be placed on the market and/or put into service only if they comply with the requirements laid down in this Directive when duly supplied, properly implanted and/or properly installed, maintained and used in accordance with their intended purposes.’;</P>
<P class="p86 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft66">Article 3 shall be replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p327 ft3">‘Article 3</P>
<P class="p375 ft27">The active implantable medical devices referred to in Article 1(2)(c), (d) and (e), hereinafter referred to as “devices”, shall satisfy the essential requirements set out in Annex 1 which apply to them, account being taken of the intended purpose of the devices concerned.</P>
<P class="p792 ft27">Where a relevant hazard exists, devices which are also machinery within the meaning of Article 2(a) of Directive 2006/42/EC of the European Parliament and of the Council of 17 May 2006 on machinery (*) shall also meet the essential health and safety requirements set out in Annex I to that Directive to the extent to which those essential health and safety requirements are more specific than the essential requirements set out in Annex 1 to this Directive.</P>
<P class="p791 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(*)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft73">OJ L 157, 9.6.2006, p. 24.’;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p793 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft66">in Article 4, paragraphs 1, 2 and 3 shall be replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p794 ft2">‘1. Member States shall not create any obstacle to the placing on the market or the putting into service within their territory of devices complying with the provisions of this Directive and bearing the CE marking provided for in Article 12, which indicates that they have been the subject of an assessment of their conformity in accordance with Article 9.</P>
<P class="p485 ft2">2. Member States shall not create any obstacles to:</P>
<P class="p795 ft27"><SPAN class="ft27">—</SPAN><SPAN class="ft75">devices intended for clinical investigations being made available to duly qualified medical practitioners or authorised persons for that purpose if they satisfy the conditions laid down in Article 10 and in Annex 6,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p796 ft2"><SPAN class="ft27">—</SPAN><NOBR><SPAN class="ft73">custom-made</SPAN></NOBR> devices being placed on the market and put into service if they satisfy the conditions laid down in Annex 6 and are accompanied by the statement, which shall be available to the particular identified patient, referred to in that Annex.</P>
<P class="p334 ft2">These devices shall not bear the CE marking.</P>

<P class="p86 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">7.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft66">Article 8 shall be replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p290 ft3">‘Article 8</P>
<P class="p805 ft27">1. Member States shall take the necessary steps to ensure that information brought to their knowledge regarding the incidents mentioned below involving a device is recorded and evaluated in a centralised manner:</P>
<P class="p806 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft73">any malfunction of or deterioration in the character­ istics and performances of a device, as well as any inadequacy in the labelling or in the instructions for use which might lead to or might have led to the death of a patient or user or to a serious deterioration in his state of health;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p807 ft27"><SPAN class="ft23">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft55">any technical or medical reason in relation to the characteristics or performances of a device for the reasons referred to in point (a), leading to systematic recall of devices of the same type by the manufacturer.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p808 ft27"><SPAN class="ft27">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft82">Where a Member State requires medical practitioners or the medical institutions to inform the competent authorities of any incidents referred to in paragraph 1, it shall take the necessary steps to ensure that the manufacturer of the device concerned, or his authorised representative, is also informed of the incident.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p809 ft52"><SPAN class="ft52">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft84">After carrying out an assessment, if possible together with the manufacturer or his authorised representative, Member States shall, without prejudice to Article 7, immediately inform the Commission and the other Member States of measures that have been taken or are contemplated to minimise the recurrence of the incidents referred to in paragraph 1, including information on the underlying incidents.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p810 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft81">The measures necessary for the implementation of this Article shall be adopted in accordance with the regulatory procedure referred to in Article 6(3).’;</SPAN></P>

<P class="p821 ft52">5. Clinical investigations shall be conducted in accordance with the provisions of Annex 7. <P class="p212 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">11.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft85">the following Articles shall be inserted:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p334 ft3">‘Article 10a</P>
<P class="p822 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft81">Any manufacturer who, under his own name, places devices on the market in accordance with the procedure referred to in Article 9(2) shall inform the competent authorities of the Member State in which he has his registered place of business of the address of the registered place of business and the description of the devices concerned.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p408 ft2">Member States may request to be informed of all data allowing for the devices to be identified together with the label and the instructions for use when the devices are put into service within their territory.</P>
<P class="p823 ft27"><SPAN class="ft27">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft82">Where a manufacturer who places a device on the market under his own name does not have a registered place of business in a Member State, he shall designate a single authorised representative in the European Union.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p824 ft2">For devices referred to in the first subparagraph of paragraph 1 the authorised representative shall inform the competent authority of the Member State in which he has his registered place of business of all details as referred to in paragraph 1.</P>
<P class="p823 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft81">The Member States shall on request inform the other Member States and the Commission of the details referred to in the first subparagraph of paragraph 1 given by the manufacturer or authorised representative.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p354 ft3">Article 10b</P>
<P class="p490 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft81">Regulatory data in accordance with this Directive shall be stored in a European databank accessible to the competent authorities to enable them to carry out their tasks relating to this Directive on a </SPAN><NOBR>well-informed</NOBR> basis.</P>

<P class="p21 ft2">The databank shall contain the following:</P>
<P class="p825 ft27"><SPAN class="ft16">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft55">data relating to certificates issued, modified, supple­ mented, suspended, withdrawn or refused according to the procedures as laid down in Annexes 2 to 5;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p826 ft2"><SPAN class="ft23">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft86">data obtained in accordance with the vigilance procedure as defined in Article 8;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p827 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft49">data relating to clinical investigations referred to in Article 10.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p354 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft86">Data shall be forwarded in a standardised format.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p828 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft86">The measures necessary for the implementation of paragraphs 1 and 2 of this Article, in particular paragraph 1 (c), shall be adopted in accordance with the regulatory procedure referred to in Article 6(3).</SPAN></P>
<P class="p339 ft3">Article 10c</P>
<P class="p829 ft27">Where a Member State considers in relation to a given product or group of products that, in order to ensure protection of health and safety and/or to ensure that public health requirements are observed, such products should be withdrawn from the market, or their placing on the market and putting into service should be prohibited, restricted or subjected to particular requirements, it may take any necessary and justified transitional measures.</P>
<P class="p403 ft2">The Member State shall then inform the Commission and all the other Member States of the transitional measures, giving the reasons for its decision.</P>
<P class="p830 ft27">The Commission shall, whenever possible, consult the interested Parties and the Member States. The Commission shall adopt its opinion, indicating whether the national measures are justified or not. The Commission shall inform all the Member States and the consulted interested Parties.</P>
<P class="p831 ft61">When appropriate, the necessary measures designed to amend <NOBR>non-essential</NOBR> elements of this Directive, by supplementing it, relating to withdrawal from the market, prohibition of placing on the market and putting into service of a certain product or group of products or to restrictions or introduction of particular requirements therefor, shall be adopted in accordance with the regulatory procedure with scrutiny referred to in Article 6(4). On imperative grounds of urgency, the Commission may use the urgency procedure referred to in Article 6(5).’;</P>
<P class="p108 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">12.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft85">Article 11 shall be amended as follows:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p832 ft52"><SPAN class="ft16">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft118">in paragraph 2, the following subparagraph shall be added: ‘When appropriate in the light of technical progress, the detailed measures necessary to ensure a consistent application of the criteria set out in Annex 8 to this Directive for the designation of bodies by the Member States shall be adopted in accordance with the regulatory procedure referred to in Article 6(3).’;</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p387 ft2"><SPAN class="ft23">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft49">in paragraph 4, the words ‘agent established in the Community’ shall be replaced by the words ‘authorised representative’;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p334 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft73">the following paragraphs shall be added:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p465 ft61">‘5. The notified body shall inform its competent authority about all certificates issued, modified, supplemented, suspended, withdrawn or refused and the other notified bodies within the scope of this Directive about certificates suspended, withdrawn or refused and, on request, about certificates issued. The notified body shall also make available, on request, all additional relevant information.</P>
<P class="p833 ft61">6. Where a notified body finds that pertinent requirements of this Directive have not been met or are no longer met by the manufacturer or that a certificate should not have been issued, it shall, taking account of the principle of proportionality, suspend or withdraw the certificate issued or place any restrictions on it unless compliance with such requirements is ensured by the implementation of appropriate corrective measures by the manufacturer.</P>
<P class="p834 ft2">In the case of suspension or withdrawal of the certificate or of any restriction placed on it or in cases where an intervention of the competent authority may become necessary, the notified body shall inform its competent authority thereof.</P>
<P class="p811 ft2">The Member State shall inform the other Member States and the Commission.</P>
<P class="p835 ft2">7. The notified body shall, on request, supply all relevant information and documents, including bud­ getary documents, required to enable the Member State to verify compliance with the criteria laid down in Annex 8.’;</P>
<P class="p132 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">13.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft85">Article 13 shall be replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>

<P class="p836 ft27"><SPAN class="ft16">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft75">where a Member State establishes that the CE marking has been affixed unduly or is missing in violation of this Directive, the manufacturer or his authorised representative established within the Community shall be obliged to end the infringement under conditions imposed by the Member State;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p837 ft2"><SPAN class="ft23">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft49">where </SPAN><NOBR>non-compliance</NOBR> continues, the Member State must take all appropriate measures to restrict or prohibit the placing on the market of the device in question or to ensure that it is withdrawn from the market in accordance with the procedures laid down in Article 7.</P>

<P class="p337 ft2"><SPAN class="ft23">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft86">paragraph 3 shall be replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p883 ft27">‘3. After carrying out an assessment, if possible together with the manufacturer or his authorised representative, Member States shall, without prejudice to Article 8, immediately inform the Commission and the other Member States of measures that have been taken or are contemplated to minimise the recurrence of the incidents referred to in paragraph 1, including information on the underlying incidents.’;</P>
<P class="p339 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft49">the following paragraph shall be added:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p884 ft2">‘4. Any appropriate measures to adopt procedures to implement this Article shall be adopted in accordance with the regulatory procedure referred to in Article 7(2).’;</P>
<P class="p132 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">9.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft66">Article 11 shall be amended as follows:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p882 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft49">in paragraphs 8 and 9 the words ‘established in the Community’ shall be deleted;</SPAN></P>

</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p21 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft73">the following paragraph shall be added:</SPAN></P>

<P class="p488 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">10.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft85">Article 12 shall be amended as follows:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p886 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft73">the title shall be replaced by ‘Particular procedure for systems and procedure packs and procedure for sterilisation’;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p329 ft2"><SPAN class="ft23">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft49">paragraph 3 shall be replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p887 ft52">‘3. Any natural or legal person who sterilises, for the purpose of placing on the market, systems or procedure packs referred to in paragraph 2 or other <NOBR>CE-marked</NOBR> medical devices designed by their manu­ facturers to be sterilised before use, shall, at his choice, follow one of the procedures referred to in Annex II or V. The application of the abovementioned Annexes and the intervention of the notified body are limited to the aspects of the procedure relating to the obtaining of sterility until the sterile package is opened or damaged. The person shall draw up a declaration stating that sterilisation has been carried out in accordance with the manufacturer's instruc­ tions.’;</P>
<P class="p888 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft73">in paragraph 4, the third sentence shall be replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p889 ft2">‘The declarations referred to in paragraphs 2 and 3 shall be kept at the disposal of the competent authorities for a period of five years.’;</P>
<P class="p108 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">11.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft85">The following Article shall be inserted:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p464 ft3">‘Article 12a</P>
<P class="p339 ft12">Reprocessing of medical devices</P>
<P class="p890 ft2">The Commission shall, no later than 5 September 2010, submit a report to the European Parliament and to the Council on the issue of the reprocessing of medical devices in the Community.</P>
<P class="p891 ft27">In the light of the findings of this report, the Commission shall submit to the European Parliament and to the Council any additional proposal it may deem appropriate in order to ensure a high level of health protection.’</P>

<P class="p513 ft2">1. A Member State shall submit a duly substantiated request to the Commission and ask it to take the necessary measures in the following situations:</P>
<P class="p894 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft73">that Member State considers that the application of the classification rules set out in Annex IX requires a decision with regard to the classification of a given device or category of devices;</SPAN></P>

<P class="p896 ft61"><SPAN class="ft23">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft60">that Member State considers that a decision is required as to whether a particular product or product group falls within one of the definitions in Article 1(2)(a) to</SPAN></P>

<P class="p898 ft2">2. The Commission shall inform the Member States of the measures taken.’;</P>
<P class="p765 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">13.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft85">Article 14 shall be amended as follows:</SPAN></P>

<P class="p132 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">15.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft85">Article 14b shall be replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p339 ft3">‘Article 14b</P>
<P class="p907 ft12">Particular health monitoring measures</P>
<P class="p908 ft61">Where a Member State considers, in relation to a given product or group of products, that, in order to ensure protection of health and safety and/or to ensure that public health requirements are observed, such products should be withdrawn from the market, or their placing on the market and putting into service should be prohibited, restricted or subjected to particular requirements, it may take any necessary and justified transitional measures.</P>
<P class="p792 ft27">The Member State shall then inform the Commission and all other Member States, giving the reasons for its decision.</P>
<P class="p909 ft2">The Commission shall, whenever possible, consult the interested Parties and the Member States.</P>
<P class="p330 ft2">The Commission shall adopt its opinion, indicating whether the national measures are justified or not. The Commission shall inform all the Member States and the consulted interested Parties thereof.</P>

<P class="p910 ft27">(3). On imperative grounds of urgency, the Commission may use the urgency procedure referred to in Article 7(4).’;</P>
<P class="p238 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">16.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft85">Article 15 shall be amended as follows:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p911 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft49">paragraphs 1, 2 and 3 shall be replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p912 ft52">‘1. In the case of devices intended for clinical investigations, the manufacturer or the authorised representative, established in the Community, shall follow the procedure referred to in Annex VIII and notify the competent authorities of the Member States in which the investigations are to be conducted by means of the statement mentioned in Section 2.2 of Annex VIII.</P>
<P class="p913 ft2">2. In the case of devices falling within Class III and implantable and <NOBR>long-term</NOBR> invasive devices falling within Class IIa or IIb, the manufacturer may commence the relevant clinical investigation at the end of a period of 60 days after notification, unless the competent authorities have notified him within that period of a decision to the contrary based on considerations of public health or public policy.</P>
<P class="p914 ft2">Member States may however authorise manufacturers to commence the relevant clinical investigations before the expiry of the period of 60 days, insofar as the relevant ethics committee has issued a favourable opinion on the programme of investigation in question, including its review of the clinical investigation plan.</P>
<P class="p915 ft52"><SPAN class="ft52">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft84">In the case of devices other than those referred to in paragraph 2, Member States may authorise manufacturers to commence clinical investigations immediately after the date of notification, provided that the ethics committee concerned has issued a favourable opinion on the programme of investigation in question including its review of the clinical investigation plan.’;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p380 ft2"><SPAN class="ft23">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft86">paragraphs 5, 6 and 7 shall be replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p912 ft52">‘5. The clinical investigations must be conducted in accordance with the provisions of Annex X. The measures designed to amend <NOBR>non-essential</NOBR> elements of this Directive, inter alia by supplementing it, relating to the provisions on clinical investigation in Annex X shall be adopted in accordance with the regulatory procedure with scrutiny referred to in Article 7(3).</P>
<P class="p913 ft27"><SPAN class="ft27">6.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft82">The Member States shall, if necessary, take the appropriate steps to ensure public health and public policy. Where a clinical investigation is refused or</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p916 ft52">halted by a Member State, that Member State shall communicate its decision and the grounds therefor to all Member States and the Commission. Where a Member State has called for a significant modification or temporary interruption of a clinical investigation, that Member State shall inform the Member States concerned about its actions and the grounds for the actions taken.</P>
<P class="p917 ft27">7. The manufacturer or his authorised representative shall notify the competent authorities of the Member States concerned of the end of the clinical investiga­ tion, with a justification in case of early termination. In the case of early termination of the clinical investigation on safety grounds this notification shall be communicated to all Member States and the Commission. The manufacturer or his authorised representative shall keep the report referred to in Section 2.3.7 of Annex X at the disposal of the competent authorities.’;</P>
<P class="p132 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">17.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft85">Article 16 shall be amended as follows:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p918 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft73">the following subparagraph shall be added to paragraph 2:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p919 ft27">‘When appropriate in the light of technical progress, the detailed measures necessary to ensure a consistent application of the criteria set out in Annex XI for the designation of bodies by the Member States shall be adopted in accordance with the regulatory procedure referred to in Article 7(2).’;</P>
<P class="p920 ft2"><SPAN class="ft23">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft49">in paragraph 4, the words ‘established in the Community’ shall be deleted;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p471 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft73">paragraph 5 shall be replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p919 ft61">‘5. The notified body shall inform its competent authority about all certificates issued, modified, supplemented, suspended, withdrawn or refused and the other notified bodies within the scope of this Directive about certificates suspended, withdrawn or refused and, on request, about certificates issued. The notified body shall also make available, on request, all additional relevant information.’;</P>
<P class="p353 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">18.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft85">in Article 18 point (a) shall be replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p921 ft27">‘(a) where a Member State establishes that the CE marking has been affixed unduly or is missing in violation of the Directive, the manufacturer or his authorised representative shall be obliged to end the infringement under conditions imposed by the Member State;’;</P>
<P class="p922 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">19.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft85">in Article 19(2), the words ‘established in the Community’ shall be deleted;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p923 ft124"><SPAN class="ft2">20.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft122">Article 20 shall be replaced by the following: </SPAN><SPAN class="ft123">‘Article 20</SPAN></P>
<P class="p924 ft12">Confidentiality</P>
<P class="p925 ft27">1. Without prejudice to the existing national provisions and practices on medical confidentiality, Member States shall ensure that all the Parties involved in the application</P>

<DIV id="id_2">
<DIV id="id_2_1">
<P class="p396 ft2">of this Directive are bound to observe confidentiality with regard to all information obtained in carrying out their tasks.</P>
<P class="p472 ft2">This does not affect the obligation of Member States and notified bodies with regard to mutual information and the dissemination of warnings, nor the obligations of the persons concerned to provide information under criminal law.</P>
<P class="p926 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft86">The following information shall not be treated as confidential:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p895 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft73">information on the registration of persons responsible for placing devices on the market in accordance with Article 14;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p895 ft2"><SPAN class="ft23">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft49">information to users sent out by the manufacturer, authorised representative or distributor in relation to a measure according to Article 10(3);</SPAN></P>
<P class="p509 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft73">information contained in certificates issued, modified, supplemented, suspended or withdrawn.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p383 ft61">3. The measures designed to amend <NOBR>non-essential</NOBR> elements of this Directive, <SPAN class="ft71">inter alia </SPAN>by supplementing it, relating to determination of the conditions under which other information may be made publicly available, and in particular for Class IIb and Class III devices to any obligation for manufacturers to prepare and make available a summary of the information and data related to the device, shall be adopted in accordance with the regulatory procedure with scrutiny referred to in Article 7(3).’;</P>
<P class="p927 ft96"><SPAN class="ft2">21.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft94">the following Article shall be inserted: </SPAN><SPAN class="ft95">‘Article 20a</SPAN></P>
<P class="p512 ft12">Cooperation</P>
<P class="p928 ft27">Member States shall take appropriate measures to ensure that the competent authorities of the Member States cooperate with each other and with the Commission and transmit to each other the information necessary to enable this Directive to be applied uniformly.</P>
<P class="p514 ft2">The Commission shall provide for the organisation of an exchange of experience between the competent authorities responsible for market surveillance in order to coordinate the uniform application of this Directive.</P>
<P class="p514 ft2">Without prejudice to the provisions of this Directive, cooperation may be part of initiatives developed at an international level.’;</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p516 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">22.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft85">Annexes I to X shall be amended in accordance with Annex II to this Directive.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p929 ft3">Article 3</P>
<P class="p930 ft2">In Article 1(2) of Directive 98/8/EC the following point shall be added:</P>
<P class="p931 ft2">‘(s) Directive 98/79/EC of the European Parliament and of the Council of 27 October 1998 on in vitro diagnostic medical devices (*).</P>
<P class="p932 ft2"><SPAN class="ft16">(*)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft73">OJ L 331, 7.12.1998, p. 1. Directive as last amended by Regulation (EC) No 1882/2003 (OJ L 284, 31.10.2003, p. 1).’</SPAN></P>
<P class="p929 ft3">Article 4</P>
<P class="p933 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft86">Member States shall adopt and publish by 21 December 2008 the laws, regulations and administrative provisions necessary to comply with this Directive. They shall forthwith communicate to the Commission the text of those measures.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p353 ft2">They shall apply those measures from 21 March 2010.</P>
<P class="p934 ft27">When Member States adopt those measures, they shall contain a reference to this Directive or be accompanied by such a reference on the occasion of their official publication. The methods of making such reference shall be laid down by Member States.</P>
<P class="p935 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft86">Member States shall communicate to the Commission the text of the main provisions of national law which they adopt in the field covered by this Directive.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p936 ft3">Article 5</P>
<P class="p937 ft27">This Directive shall enter into force on the 20th day following its publication in the <SPAN class="ft25">Official Journal of the European Union</SPAN>.</P>
<P class="p938 ft3">Article 6</P>
<P class="p235 ft2">This Directive is addressed to the Member States.</P>
<P class="p107 ft2">Done at Strasbourg, 5 September 2007.</P>

<P class="p531 ft98">ANNEX I</P>
<P class="p532 ft23">Annexes 1 to 7 to Directive 90/385/EEC shall be amended as follows:</P>
<P class="p533 ft23"><SPAN class="ft16">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft99">Annex 1 shall be amended as follows:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p534 ft23"><SPAN class="ft16">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft102">the following Section shall be inserted:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p567 ft23">‘5a. Demonstration of conformity with the essential requirements must include a clinical evaluation in accordance with Annex 7.’;</P>
<P class="p536 ft23"><SPAN class="ft16">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft105">in Section 8, the fifth indent shall be replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p537 ft57">‘— risks connected with ionising radiation from radioactive substances included in the device, in compliance with the protection requirements laid down in Council Directive 96/29/Euratom of 13 May 1996 laying down basic safety standards for the protection of the health of workers and the general public against the dangers arising from ionising radiation (*) and Council Directive 97/43/Euratom of 30 June 1997 on health protection of individuals against the dangers of ionising radiation in relation to medical exposure (**).</P>
<P class="p538 ft23"><SPAN class="ft101">(*)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft102">OJ L 159, 29.6.1996, p. 1.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p539 ft23"><SPAN class="ft101">(**)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft103">OJ L 180, 9.7.1997, p. 22.’;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p536 ft23"><SPAN class="ft16">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft102">in Section 9, seventh indent, the following phrase shall be added:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p540 ft23">‘For devices which incorporate software or which are medical software in themselves, the software must be validated according to the state of the art taking into account the principles of development lifecycle, risk management, validation and verification.’;</P>
<P class="p541 ft23"><SPAN class="ft16">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft105">Section 10 shall be replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p941 ft59">‘10. Where a device incorporates, as an integral part, a substance which, if used separately, may be considered to be a medicinal product as defined in Article 1 of Directive 2001/83/EC, and which is liable to act upon the body with action ancillary to that of the device, the quality, safety and usefulness of the substance must be verified by analogy with the methods specified in Annex I to Directive 2001/83/EC.</P>
<P class="p942 ft59">For the substances referred to in the first paragraph, the notified body shall, having verified the usefulness of the substance as part of the medical device and taking account of the intended purpose of the device, seek a scientific opinion from one of the competent authorities designated by the Member States or the European Medicines Agency (EMEA) acting particularly through its committee in accordance with Regulation (EC) No 726/2004 (*) on the quality and safety of the substance including the clinical benefit/ risk profile of the incorporation of the substance into the device. When issuing its opinion, the competent authority or the EMEA shall take into account the manufacturing process and the data related to the usefulness of incorporation of the substance into the device as determined by the notified body.</P>
<P class="p588 ft57">Where a device incorporates, as an integral part, a human blood derivative, the notified body shall, having verified the usefulness of the substance as part of the device and taking account of the intended purpose of the device, seek a scientific opinion from the EMEA, acting particularly through its committee, on the quality and safety of the substance, including the clinical benefit/risk profile of the incorporation of the human blood derivative into the device. When issuing its opinion, the EMEA shall take into account the manufacturing process and the data related to the usefulness of incorporation of the substance into the device as determined by the notified body.</P>
<P class="p546 ft59">Where changes are made to an ancillary substance incorporated in a device, in particular related to its manufacturing process, the notified body shall be informed of the changes and shall consult the relevant medicines competent authority (i.e. the one involved in the initial consultation), in order to confirm that the quality and safety of the ancillary substance are maintained. The competent authority shall take into account the data related to the usefulness of the incorporation of the substance into the device as determined by the notified body, in order to ensure that the changes have no negative impact on the established benefit/risk profile of the addition of the substance in the device.</P>
<P class="p943 ft59">When the relevant medicines competent authority (i.e. the one involved in the initial consultation) has obtained information on the ancillary substance, which could have an impact on the established benefit/ risk profile of the addition of the substance to the device, it shall provide the notified body with advice,</P>

The notified body shall take the updated scientific opinion into account in reconsidering its assessment of the conformity assessment procedure.</P>

Regulation as last amended by Regulation (EC) No 1901/2006.’;</SPAN></P>

<P class="p550 ft23"><SPAN class="ft101">(iii)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft103">the following indent shall be inserted after the fourth indent:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p696 ft23">‘— if the device incorporates, as an integral part, a substance or human blood derivative referred to in Section 10 of Annex 1, the data on the tests conducted in this connection which are required to assess the safety, quality and usefulness of that substance, or human blood derivative, taking account of the intended purpose of the device,’;</P>
<P class="p541 ft23"><SPAN class="ft16">(e)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft102">the following two sections shall be added:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p598 ft23">‘4. The information included in the declarations covered by this Annex shall be kept for a period of at least 15 years from the date of manufacture of the last product.</P>
<P class="p962 ft23"><SPAN class="ft16">5.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft99">For </SPAN><NOBR>custom-made</NOBR> devices, the manufacturer must undertake to review and to document experience gained in the <NOBR>post-production</NOBR> phase, including the provisions referred to in Annex 7, and to implement appropriate means to apply any necessary corrective action. This undertaking must include an obligation for the manufacturer to notify the competent authorities of the following incidents immediately on learning of them and the relevant corrective actions:</P>
<P class="p963 ft23"><SPAN class="ft16">(i)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft99">any malfunction or deterioration in the characteristics and/or performance of a device, as well as any inadequacy in the labelling or the instructions for use which might lead to or might have led to the death of a patient or user or to a serious deterioration in his state of health;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p619 ft23"><SPAN class="ft101">(ii)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft102">any technical or medical reason connected with the characteristics or performance of a device for the reasons referred to in point (i) leading to systematic recall of devices of the same type by the manufacturer.’;</SPAN></P>

<P class="p579 ft23"><SPAN class="ft16">7.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft99">Annex 7 shall be amended as follows:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p549 ft23"><SPAN class="ft16">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft102">Section 1 shall be replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p602 ft53"><SPAN class="ft23">‘1. </SPAN>General provisions</P>
<P class="p964 ft57"><SPAN class="ft16">1.1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft106">As a general rule, confirmation of conformity with the requirements concerning the characteristics and performances referred to in Sections 1 and 2 of Annex 1 under the normal conditions of use of the device and the evaluation of the </SPAN><NOBR>side-effects</NOBR> and of the acceptability of the benefit/risk ratio referred to in Section 5 of Annex 1, must be based on clinical data. The evaluation of this data (hereinafter referred to as clinical evaluation), where appropriate taking account of any relevant harmonised standards, must follow a defined and methodologically sound procedure based on:</P>
<P class="p604 ft23"><SPAN class="ft16">1.1.1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft125">Either a critical evaluation of the relevant scientific literature currently available relating to the safety, performance, design characteristics and intended purpose of the device where:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p605 ft23"><SPAN class="ft16">—</SPAN><SPAN class="ft102">there is demonstration of equivalence of the device to the device to which the data relates and,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p606 ft23"><SPAN class="ft16">—</SPAN><SPAN class="ft102">the data adequately demonstrate compliance with the relevant essential requirements;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p607 ft23"><SPAN class="ft16">1.1.2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft125">Or a critical evaluation of the results of all the clinical investigations made,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p591 ft23"><SPAN class="ft16">1.1.3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft125">Or a critical evaluation of the combined clinical data provided in 1.1.1 and 1.1.2.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p607 ft23"><SPAN class="ft16">1.2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft99">Clinical investigations shall be performed unless it is duly justified to rely on existing clinical data.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p965 ft23"><SPAN class="ft16">1.3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft99">The clinical evaluation and its outcome shall be documented. This documentation shall be included and/or fully referenced in the technical documentation of the device.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p966 ft23"><SPAN class="ft16">1.4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft99">The clinical evaluation and its documentation must be actively updated with data obtained from the </SPAN><NOBR>post-market</NOBR> surveillance. Where <NOBR>post-market</NOBR> clinical <NOBR>follow-up</NOBR> as part of the <NOBR>post-market</NOBR> surveillance plan for the device is not deemed necessary, this must be duly justified and documented.</P>
<P class="p967 ft57"><SPAN class="ft16">1.5.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft106">Where demonstration of conformity with essential requirements based on clinical data is not deemed appropriate, adequate justification for any such exclusion has to be given based on risk management output and under consideration of the specifics of the device/body interaction, the clinical performances intended and the claims of the manufacturer. Adequacy of demonstration of conformity with the essential requirements by performance evaluation, bench testing and </SPAN><NOBR>pre-clinical</NOBR> evaluation alone has to be duly substantiated.</P>
<P class="p552 ft23"><SPAN class="ft16">1.6.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft99">All data must remain confidential unless it is deemed essential that they be divulged.’</SPAN></P>
<P class="p549 ft23"><SPAN class="ft16">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft105">Section 2.3.5 shall be replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p968 ft23">‘2.3.5. All serious adverse events must be fully recorded and immediately notified to all competent authorities of the Member States in which the clinical investigation is being performed.’</P>
<P class="p969 ft23"><SPAN class="ft16">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft102">In Section 2.3.6, the words ‘appropriately qualified medical specialist’ shall be replaced by the words ‘duly qualified medical practitioner or authorised person’.</SPAN></P>

<P class="p970 ft98">ANNEX II</P>
<P class="p532 ft23">Annexes I to X to Directive 93/42/EEC shall be amended as follows:</P>
<P class="p954 ft23"><SPAN class="ft16">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft99">Annex I shall be amended as follows:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p597 ft23"><SPAN class="ft16">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft102">Section 1 shall be replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p971 ft57">‘1. The devices must be designed and manufactured in such a way that, when used under the conditions and for the purposes intended, they will not compromise the clinical condition or the safety of patients, or the safety and health of users or, where applicable, other persons, provided that any risks which may be associated with their intended use constitute acceptable risks when weighed against the benefits to the patient and are compatible with a high level of protection of health and safety.</P>
<P class="p711 ft23">This shall include:</P>
<P class="p972 ft23"><SPAN class="ft23">—</SPAN><SPAN class="ft102">reducing, as far as possible, the risk of use error due to the ergonomic features of the device and the environment in which the device is intended to be used (design for patient safety), and</SPAN></P>
<P class="p593 ft23"><SPAN class="ft23">—</SPAN><SPAN class="ft102">consideration of the technical knowledge, experience, education and training and where applicable the medical and physical conditions of intended users (design for lay, professional, disabled or other users).’;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p534 ft23"><SPAN class="ft16">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft105">the following Section shall be inserted:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p973 ft23">‘6a. Demonstration of conformity with the essential requirements must include a clinical evaluation in accordance with Annex X.’;</P>
<P class="p566 ft23"><SPAN class="ft16">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft102">in Section 7.1, the following indent shall be added:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p974 ft23">‘— where appropriate, the results of biophysical or modelling research whose validity has been demonstrated beforehand.’;</P>
<P class="p566 ft23"><SPAN class="ft16">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft105">Section 7.4. shall be replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p975 ft59">‘7.4. Where a device incorporates, as an integral part, a substance which, if used separately, may be considered to be a medicinal product as defined in Article 1 of Directive 2001/83/EC and which is liable to act upon the body with action ancillary to that of the device, the quality, safety and usefulness of the substance must be verified by analogy with the methods specified in Annex I to Directive 2001/83/EC.</P>
<P class="p976 ft59">For the substances referred to in the first paragraph, the notified body shall, having verified the usefulness of the substance as part of the medical device and taking account of the intended purpose of the device, seek a scientific opinion from one of the competent authorities designated by the Member States or the European Medicines Agency (EMEA) acting particularly through its committee in accordance with Regulation (EC) No 726/2004 (*) on the quality and safety of the substance including the clinical benefit/ risk profile of the incorporation of the substance into the device. When issuing its opinion, the competent authority or the EMEA shall take into account the manufacturing process and the data related to the usefulness of incorporation of the substance into the device as determined by the notified body.</P>
<P class="p635 ft57">Where a device incorporates, as an integral part, a human blood derivative, the notified body shall, having verified the usefulness of the substance as part of the medical device and taking into account the intended purpose of the device, seek a scientific opinion from the EMEA, acting particularly through its committee, on the quality and safety of the substance including the clinical benefit/risk profile of the incorporation of the human blood derivative into the device. When issuing its opinion, the EMEA shall take into account the manufacturing process and the data related to the usefulness of incorporation of the substance into the device as determined by the notified body.</P>
<P class="p977 ft59">Where changes are made to an ancillary substance incorporated in a device, in particular related to its manufacturing process, the notified body shall be informed of the changes and shall consult the relevant medicines competent authority (i.e. the one involved in the initial consultation), in order to confirm that the quality and safety of the ancillary substance are maintained. The competent authority shall take into</P>

<P class="p562 ft23">account the data related to the usefulness of incorporation of the substance into the device as determined by the notified body, in order to ensure that the changes have no negative impact on the established benefit/risk profile of the addition of the substance in the medical device.</P>
<P class="p978 ft59">When the relevant medicines competent authority (i.e. the one involved in the initial consultation) has obtained information on the ancillary substance, which could have an impact on the established benefit/ risk profile of the addition of the substance in the medical device, it shall provide the notified body with advice, whether this information has an impact on the established benefit/risk profile of the addition of the substance in the medical device or not. <P class="p979 ft23"><SPAN class="ft101">(*)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft102">Regulation (EC) No 726/2004 of the European Parliament and of the Council of 31 March 2004 laying down Community procedures for the authorisation and supervision of medicinal products for human and veterinary use and establishing a European Medicines Agency (OJ L 136, 30.4.2004, p. 1). Regulation as last amended by Regulation (EC) No 1901/2006.’</SPAN></P>
<P class="p534 ft23"><SPAN class="ft16">(e)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft102">Section 7.5 shall be replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p980 ft57">‘7.5. The devices must be designed and manufactured in such a way as to reduce to a minimum the risks posed by substances leaking from the device. Special attention shall be given to substances which are carcinogenic, mutagenic or toxic to reproduction, in accordance with Annex I to Council Directive 67/ 548/EEC of 27 June 1967 on the approximation of laws, regulations and administrative provisions relating to the classification, packaging and labelling of dangerous substances (*).</P>
<P class="p981 ft57">If parts of a device (or a device itself) intended to administer and/or remove medicines, body liquids or other substances to or from the body, or devices intended for transport and storage of such body fluids or substances, contain phthalates which are classified as carcinogenic, mutagenic or toxic to reproduction, of category 1 or 2, in accordance with Annex I to Directive 67/548/EEC, these devices must be labelled on the device itself and/or on the packaging for each unit or, where appropriate, on the sales packaging as a device containing phthalates.</P>
<P class="p982 ft23">If the intended use of such devices includes treatment of children or treatment of pregnant or nursing women, the manufacturer must provide a specific justification for the use of these substances with regard to compliance with the essential requirements, in particular of this paragraph, within the technical documentation and, within the instructions for use, information on residual risks for these patient groups and, if applicable, on appropriate precautionary measures.</P>
<P class="p983 ft23"><SPAN class="ft101">(*)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft102">OJ 196, 16.8.1967, p. 1. Directive as last amended by Directive 2006/121/EC of the European Parliament and of the Council (OJ L 396, 30.12.2006, p. 850).’</SPAN></P>
<P class="p597 ft23"><SPAN class="ft16">(f)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft99">in Section 8.2, the word ‘transferable’ shall be replaced by the word ‘transmissible’;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p685 ft23"><SPAN class="ft16">(g)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft102">the following Section shall be inserted:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p632 ft23">‘12.1a For devices which incorporate software or which are medical software in themselves, the software must be validated according to the state of the art taking into account the principles of development lifecycle, risk management, validation and verification.’;</P>
<P class="p597 ft23"><SPAN class="ft16">(h)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft105">in Section 13.1, the first paragraph shall be replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>

<P class="p550 ft23"><SPAN class="ft101">(iii)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft103">point (c) shall be replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
